vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.05764em;">E</span><span class="mord mathit">x</span><span class="mord mathit">t</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">r</span><span class="mord mathit">u</span><span class="mord mathit">s</span><span class="mord mathit">i</span><span class="mord mathit">o</span><span class="mord mathit">n</span></span></span></span></span> and <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>P</mi><mi>e</mi><mi>r</mi><mi>m</mi><mi>u</mi><mi>t</mi><mi>a</mi><mi>t</mi><mi>i</mi><mi>o</mi><mi>n</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">Permutation</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.13889em;">P</span><span class="mord mathit">e</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">r</span><span class="mord mathit">m</span><span class="mord mathit">u</span><span class="mord mathit">t</span><span class="mord mathit">a</span><span class="mord mathit">t</span><span class="mord mathit">i</span><span class="mord mathit">o</span><span class="mord mathit">n</span></span></span></span></span> and the extended <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo>∈</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\in</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.5391em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.5782em; vertical-align: -0.0391em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mrel">∈</span></span></span></span></span> relation.</p>
<h1 id="examples">Examples</h1>
<h2 id="graphs-as-morphism">Graphs as morphism</h2>
<p>Let <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>X</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">X</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span></span></span></span></span> be some set of variables, <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>D</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">D</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">D</span></span></span></span></span> be some domain, such as <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>N</mi><mi>a</mi><mi>t</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">Nat</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.10903em;">N</span><span class="mord mathit">a</span><span class="mord mathit">t</span></span></span></span></span>, the natural numbers, or <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>B</mi><mi>o</mi><mi>o</mi><mi>l</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">Bool</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.05017em;">B</span><span class="mord mathit">o</span><span class="mord mathit">o</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.01968em;">l</span></span></span></span></span>, the booleans. We can describe many graphs as morphisms, <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>g</mi><mo>(</mo><mi>X</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>D</mi><mo>)</mo><mo>:</mo><mi>D</mi><mo>→</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">G</mi></mrow><mo>[</mo><mi>X</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>D</mi><mo>]</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">g(X,D): D \to \mathsf{G}[X,D]</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">D</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mrel">:</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">D</span><span class="mrel">→</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">G</span></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">D</span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span>.</p>
<h3 id="the-discrete-graph">The discrete graph</h3>
<p>The discrete graph of <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>n</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">n</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathit">n</span></span></span></span></span> elements, written <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">d</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">i</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">s</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">c</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">r</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">t</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{discrete}(n)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">d</span><span class="mord mathsf">i</span><span class="mord mathsf">s</span><span class="mord mathsf">c</span><span class="mord mathsf" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">r</span><span class="mord mathsf">e</span><span class="mord mathsf">t</span><span class="mord mathsf">e</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathit">n</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span>, is simply <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>n</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">n</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathit">n</span></span></span></span></span> unconnected vertices. Noting that the graph consisting of a single vertex, <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>n</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">n</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathit">n</span></span></span></span></span>, has the form <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>n</mi><mo>→</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">n \to 0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathit">n</span><span class="mrel">→</span><span class="mord mathrm">0</span></span></span></span></span>, which adjoins <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>n</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">n</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathit">n</span></span></span></span></span> to the empty graph, <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathrm">0</span></span></span></span></span>, we can define the domain of discrete graphs recursively.</p>
<p><span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">d</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">i</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">s</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">c</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">r</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">t</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><mn>0</mn><mo>)</mo><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{discrete}(0) = 0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">d</span><span class="mord mathsf">i</span><span class="mord mathsf">s</span><span class="mord mathsf">c</span><span class="mord mathsf" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">r</span><span class="mord mathsf">e</span><span class="mord mathsf">t</span><span class="mord mathsf">e</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathrm">0</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mord mathrm">0</span></span></span></span></span><br>
<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">d</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">i</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">s</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">c</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">r</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">t</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo><mo>=</mo><mi>n</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">∣</mi><mn>0</mn><mo>⊗</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">d</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">i</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">s</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">c</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">r</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">t</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{discrete}(n) = n | 0 \otimes \mathsf{discrete}(n-1)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">d</span><span class="mord mathsf">i</span><span class="mord mathsf">s</span><span class="mord mathsf">c</span><span class="mord mathsf" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">r</span><span class="mord mathsf">e</span><span class="mord mathsf">t</span><span class="mord mathsf">e</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathit">n</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mord mathit">n</span><span class="mord mathrm">∣</span><span class="mord mathrm">0</span><span class="mbin">⊗</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">d</span><span class="mord mathsf">i</span><span class="mord mathsf">s</span><span class="mord mathsf">c</span><span class="mord mathsf" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">r</span><span class="mord mathsf">e</span><span class="mord mathsf">t</span><span class="mord mathsf">e</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathit">n</span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mord mathrm">1</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span><br>
<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo>=</mo><mo>[</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>]</mo><mo>⊗</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">d</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">i</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">s</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">c</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">r</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">t</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">= [n]\otimes \mathsf{discrete}(n-1)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathit">n</span><span class="mclose">]</span><span class="mbin">⊗</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">d</span><span class="mord mathsf">i</span><span class="mord mathsf">s</span><span class="mord mathsf">c</span><span class="mord mathsf" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">r</span><span class="mord mathsf">e</span><span class="mord mathsf">t</span><span class="mord mathsf">e</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathit">n</span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mord mathrm">1</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>Thus, <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">d</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">i</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">s</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">c</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">r</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">t</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo><mo>=</mo><mo>[</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>]</mo><mo>⊗</mo><mo>[</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>]</mo><mo>⊗</mo><mo>⋯</mo><mo>⊗</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{discrete}(n) = [n]\otimes[n-1]\otimes\cdots\otimes0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">d</span><span class="mord mathsf">i</span><span class="mord mathsf">s</span><span class="mord mathsf">c</span><span class="mord mathsf" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">r</span><span class="mord mathsf">e</span><span class="mord mathsf">t</span><span class="mord mathsf">e</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathit">n</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathit">n</span><span class="mclose">]</span><span class="mbin">⊗</span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathit">n</span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mord mathrm">1</span><span class="mclose">]</span><span class="mbin">⊗</span><span class="minner">⋯</span><span class="mbin">⊗</span><span class="mord mathrm">0</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<h3 id="domain-elements-as-variables">Domain elements as variables</h3>
<p>Sometimes it is convenient to use domain elements as variables as well as vertices; that is, it is often useful to form graphs from <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">G</mi></mrow><mo>[</mo><mi>D</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>D</mi><mo>]</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{G}[D,D]</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">G</span></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">D</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">D</span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span>. In this case, we distinguish the mention of a domain element, say <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>d</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">d</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathit">d</span></span></span></span></span>, in the role of a variable from the mention in the role of a vertex by quotation marks. Specifically, we write <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo>┌</mo><mi>d</mi><mo>┐</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\ulcorner d\urcorner</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mopen amsrm">┌</span><span class="mord mathit">d</span><span class="mclose amsrm">┐</span></span></span></span></span>  when using <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>d</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">d</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathit">d</span></span></span></span></span> as a variable versus merely <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>d</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">d</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathit">d</span></span></span></span></span> when using <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>d</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">d</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathit">d</span></span></span></span></span> as a vertex. An example in context this might look like <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">l</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">t</mi></mrow><mspace width="0.277778em"></mspace><mo>┌</mo><mi>d</mi><mo>┐</mo><mo>=</mo><mi>d</mi><mspace width="0.277778em"></mspace><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">i</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">n</mi></mrow><mspace width="0.277778em"></mspace><mi>g</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{let}\; \ulcorner d\urcorner = d \; \mathsf{in}\; g</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.88888em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">l</span><span class="mord mathsf">e</span><span class="mord mathsf">t</span></span><span class="mopen amsrm"><span class="mspace thickspace"></span><span class="mopen amsrm">┌</span></span><span class="mord mathit">d</span><span class="mclose amsrm">┐</span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mord mathit">d</span><span class="mord"><span class="mspace thickspace"></span><span class="mord mathsf">i</span><span class="mord mathsf">n</span></span><span class="mord mathit"><span class="mspace thickspace"></span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span></span></span></span></span></span>.</p>
<h3 id="the-chain">The chain</h3>
<p>Using these two ideas we can give a recursive definition of the domain of chains. As with the discrete graph, the chain of <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathrm">0</span></span></span></span></span> elements is the empty graph. The chain of a single element is not simply adjoining that element as a vertex to the empty graph. It also selects that element. Then the recursive specification creates an edge between the graph containing a single element, <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>n</mi><mo>→</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">n \to 0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathit">n</span><span class="mrel">→</span><span class="mord mathrm">0</span></span></span></span></span>, and the chain of <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>n</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">n-1</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.72777em; vertical-align: -0.08333em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathit">n</span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mord mathrm">1</span></span></span></span></span> elements by selecting the element, <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>n</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">n</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathit">n</span></span></span></span></span> and calling it <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo>┌</mo><mn>2</mn><mi>n</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>┐</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\ulcorner 2n-1\urcorner</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69224em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.77557em; vertical-align: -0.08333em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mopen amsrm">┌</span><span class="mord mathrm">2</span><span class="mord mathit">n</span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mord mathrm">1</span><span class="mclose amsrm">┐</span></span></span></span></span>, and then linking the two resulting graphs. To ensure that the result is linkable it selects the element again, this time calling it <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo>┌</mo><mn>2</mn><mi>n</mi><mo>┐</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\ulcorner 2n \urcorner</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69224em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.69224em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mopen amsrm">┌</span><span class="mord mathrm">2</span><span class="mord mathit">n</span><span class="mclose amsrm">┐</span></span></span></span></span>.</p>
<p><span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">c</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">h</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">a</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">i</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">n</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><mn>0</mn><mo>)</mo><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{chain}(0) = 0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">c</span><span class="mord mathsf">h</span><span class="mord mathsf">a</span><span class="mord mathsf">i</span><span class="mord mathsf">n</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathrm">0</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mord mathrm">0</span></span></span></span></span><br>
<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">c</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">h</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">a</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">i</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">n</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>)</mo><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">l</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">t</mi></mrow><mspace width="0.277778em"></mspace><mo>┌</mo><mn>2</mn><mo>┐</mo><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn><mspace width="0.277778em"></mspace><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">i</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">n</mi></mrow><mspace width="0.277778em"></mspace><mo>[</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>]</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{chain}(1) = \mathsf{let}\; \ulcorner 2\urcorner = 1 \; \mathsf{in}\; [1]</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">c</span><span class="mord mathsf">h</span><span class="mord mathsf">a</span><span class="mord mathsf">i</span><span class="mord mathsf">n</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathrm">1</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">l</span><span class="mord mathsf">e</span><span class="mord mathsf">t</span></span><span class="mopen amsrm"><span class="mspace thickspace"></span><span class="mopen amsrm">┌</span></span><span class="mord mathrm">2</span><span class="mclose amsrm">┐</span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mord mathrm">1</span><span class="mord"><span class="mspace thickspace"></span><span class="mord mathsf">i</span><span class="mord mathsf">n</span></span><span class="mopen"><span class="mspace thickspace"></span><span class="mopen">[</span></span><span class="mord mathrm">1</span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span><br>
<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">c</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">h</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">a</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">i</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">n</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">l</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">t</mi></mrow><mspace width="0.277778em"></mspace><mo>┌</mo><mn>2</mn><mi>n</mi><mo>┐</mo><mo>=</mo><mi>n</mi><mspace width="0.277778em"></mspace><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">i</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">n</mi></mrow><mspace width="0.277778em"></mspace><mo>(</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">l</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">t</mi></mrow><mspace width="0.277778em"></mspace><mo>┌</mo><mn>2</mn><mi>n</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>┐</mo><mo>=</mo><mi>n</mi><mspace width="0.277778em"></mspace><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">i</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">n</mi></mrow><mspace width="0.277778em"></mspace><mo>[</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>]</mo><mo separator="true">,</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">c</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">h</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">a</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">i</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">n</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>)</mo><mo>)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{chain}(n) = \mathsf{let}\; \ulcorner2n\urcorner = n \; \mathsf{in}\;(\mathsf{let}\; \ulcorner 2n-1\urcorner = n \; \mathsf{in}\; [n], \mathsf{chain}(n-1))</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">c</span><span class="mord mathsf">h</span><span class="mord mathsf">a</span><span class="mord mathsf">i</span><span class="mord mathsf">n</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathit">n</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">l</span><span class="mord mathsf">e</span><span class="mord mathsf">t</span></span><span class="mopen amsrm"><span class="mspace thickspace"></span><span class="mopen amsrm">┌</span></span><span class="mord mathrm">2</span><span class="mord mathit">n</span><span class="mclose amsrm">┐</span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mord mathit">n</span><span class="mord"><span class="mspace thickspace"></span><span class="mord mathsf">i</span><span class="mord mathsf">n</span></span><span class="mopen"><span class="mspace thickspace"></span><span class="mopen">(</span></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">l</span><span class="mord mathsf">e</span><span class="mord mathsf">t</span></span><span class="mopen amsrm"><span class="mspace thickspace"></span><span class="mopen amsrm">┌</span></span><span class="mord mathrm">2</span><span class="mord mathit">n</span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mord mathrm">1</span><span class="mclose amsrm">┐</span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mord mathit">n</span><span class="mord"><span class="mspace thickspace"></span><span class="mord mathsf">i</span><span class="mord mathsf">n</span></span><span class="mopen"><span class="mspace thickspace"></span><span class="mopen">[</span></span><span class="mord mathit">n</span><span class="mclose">]</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">c</span><span class="mord mathsf">h</span><span class="mord mathsf">a</span><span class="mord mathsf">i</span><span class="mord mathsf">n</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathit">n</span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mord mathrm">1</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>The reader can easily verify that for each <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>n</mi><mo>≥</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">n \geq 1</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.78041em; vertical-align: -0.13597em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathit">n</span><span class="mrel">≥</span><span class="mord mathrm">1</span></span></span></span></span> <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">c</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">h</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">a</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">i</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">n</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{chain}(n)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">c</span><span class="mord mathsf">h</span><span class="mord mathsf">a</span><span class="mord mathsf">i</span><span class="mord mathsf">n</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathit">n</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span> is in nominated form.</p>
<p>Here is the chain from <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mn>2</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">2</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathrm">2</span></span></span></span></span> to <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mn>1</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">1</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.64444em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.64444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathrm">1</span></span></span></span></span>.</p>
<p><span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">c</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">h</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">a</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">i</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">n</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><mn>2</mn><mo>)</mo><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">l</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">t</mi></mrow><mspace width="0.277778em"></mspace><mo>┌</mo><mn>4</mn><mo>┐</mo><mo>=</mo><mn>2</mn><mspace width="0.277778em"></mspace><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">i</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">n</mi></mrow><mspace width="0.277778em"></mspace><mo>(</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">l</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">t</mi></mrow><mspace width="0.277778em"></mspace><mo>┌</mo><mn>3</mn><mo>┐</mo><mo>=</mo><mn>2</mn><mspace width="0.277778em"></mspace><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">i</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">n</mi></mrow><mspace width="0.277778em"></mspace><mo>[</mo><mn>2</mn><mo>]</mo><mo separator="true">,</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">l</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">t</mi></mrow><mspace width="0.277778em"></mspace><mo>┌</mo><mn>2</mn><mo>┐</mo><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn><mspace width="0.277778em"></mspace><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">i</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">n</mi></mrow><mspace width="0.277778em"></mspace><mo>[</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>]</mo><mo>)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{chain}(2) = \mathsf{let}\; \ulcorner 4 \urcorner = 2 \; \mathsf{in}\; (\mathsf{let}\; \ulcorner 3 \urcorner = 2 \; \mathsf{in}\; [2], \mathsf{let}\; \ulcorner 2\urcorner = 1 \; \mathsf{in}\; [1])</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">c</span><span class="mord mathsf">h</span><span class="mord mathsf">a</span><span class="mord mathsf">i</span><span class="mord mathsf">n</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathrm">2</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">l</span><span class="mord mathsf">e</span><span class="mord mathsf">t</span></span><span class="mopen amsrm"><span class="mspace thickspace"></span><span class="mopen amsrm">┌</span></span><span class="mord mathrm">4</span><span class="mclose amsrm">┐</span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mord mathrm">2</span><span class="mord"><span class="mspace thickspace"></span><span class="mord mathsf">i</span><span class="mord mathsf">n</span></span><span class="mopen"><span class="mspace thickspace"></span><span class="mopen">(</span></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">l</span><span class="mord mathsf">e</span><span class="mord mathsf">t</span></span><span class="mopen amsrm"><span class="mspace thickspace"></span><span class="mopen amsrm">┌</span></span><span class="mord mathrm">3</span><span class="mclose amsrm">┐</span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mord mathrm">2</span><span class="mord"><span class="mspace thickspace"></span><span class="mord mathsf">i</span><span class="mord mathsf">n</span></span><span class="mopen"><span class="mspace thickspace"></span><span class="mopen">[</span></span><span class="mord mathrm">2</span><span class="mclose">]</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">l</span><span class="mord mathsf">e</span><span class="mord mathsf">t</span></span><span class="mopen amsrm"><span class="mspace thickspace"></span><span class="mopen amsrm">┌</span></span><span class="mord mathrm">2</span><span class="mclose amsrm">┐</span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mord mathrm">1</span><span class="mord"><span class="mspace thickspace"></span><span class="mord mathsf">i</span><span class="mord mathsf">n</span></span><span class="mopen"><span class="mspace thickspace"></span><span class="mopen">[</span></span><span class="mord mathrm">1</span><span class="mclose">]</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<h3 id="the-cycle">The cycle</h3>
<p>The cyclic graph of <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>n</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">n</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathit">n</span></span></span></span></span> vertices and <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>n</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">n</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.43056em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathit">n</span></span></span></span></span> edges simply creates an additional edge from the end of the <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">c</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">h</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">a</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">i</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">n</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{chain}(n)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">c</span><span class="mord mathsf">h</span><span class="mord mathsf">a</span><span class="mord mathsf">i</span><span class="mord mathsf">n</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathit">n</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span> back to the beginning.</p>
<p><span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">c</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">y</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">c</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">l</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><mn>0</mn><mo>)</mo><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{cycle}(0) = 0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">c</span><span class="mord mathsf" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">y</span><span class="mord mathsf">c</span><span class="mord mathsf">l</span><span class="mord mathsf">e</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathrm">0</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mord mathrm">0</span></span></span></span></span><br>
<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">c</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">y</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">c</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">l</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo><mo>=</mo><mo>⟨</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">c</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">h</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">a</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">i</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">n</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo><mo separator="true">,</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">c</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">h</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">a</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">i</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">n</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>)</mo><mo>⟩</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{cycle}(n) = \langle \mathsf{chain}(n), \mathsf{chain}(1) \rangle</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">c</span><span class="mord mathsf" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">y</span><span class="mord mathsf">c</span><span class="mord mathsf">l</span><span class="mord mathsf">e</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathit">n</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mopen">⟨</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">c</span><span class="mord mathsf">h</span><span class="mord mathsf">a</span><span class="mord mathsf">i</span><span class="mord mathsf">n</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathit">n</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">c</span><span class="mord mathsf">h</span><span class="mord mathsf">a</span><span class="mord mathsf">i</span><span class="mord mathsf">n</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathrm">1</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mclose">⟩</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<h3 id="the-complete-graph">The complete graph</h3>
<p>This next example is made even more compact if we admit some syntactic sugar. First, let us stipulate that <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>D</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">D</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">D</span></span></span></span></span> supports a means of checking elements, such as <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>d</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">d</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathit">d</span></span></span></span></span>, for properties, say <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>p</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">p</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathit">p</span></span></span></span></span>, and write <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>p</mi><mo>(</mo><mi>d</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">p(d)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathit">p</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathit">d</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span> for the predicate that determines when <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>d</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">d</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathit">d</span></span></span></span></span> inhabits the property <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>p</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">p</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathit">p</span></span></span></span></span>. We can lift the edge expression to an expression between collections of elements from <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>D</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">D</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">D</span></span></span></span></span>. Specifically, we can form</p>
<p><span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo>⟨</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">f</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">o</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">r</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><msub><mi>x</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>←</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">v</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>)</mo><mspace width="0.277778em"></mspace><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">i</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">f</mi></mrow><mspace width="0.277778em"></mspace><msub><mi>p</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>(</mo><msub><mi>x</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>)</mo><mo>)</mo><mo>{</mo><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>}</mo><mo separator="true">,</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">f</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">o</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">r</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>y</mi><mo>←</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">v</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>)</mo><mspace width="0.277778em"></mspace><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">i</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">f</mi></mrow><mspace width="0.277778em"></mspace><msub><mi>p</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>(</mo><msub><mi>x</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>)</mo><mo>)</mo><mo>{</mo><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>}</mo><mo>⟩</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\langle \mathsf{for} ( x_1 \leftarrow \mathsf{v}(g_1)\; \mathsf{if}\; p_1(x_1) )\{ g_1 \}, \mathsf{for} ( y \leftarrow \mathsf{v}(g_2)\; \mathsf{if}\; p_2(x_2) )\{ g_2 \} \rangle</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mopen">⟨</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf" style="margin-right: 0.06944em;">f</span><span class="mord mathsf">o</span><span class="mord mathsf" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">r</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit">x</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mrel">←</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">v</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.03588em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mord"><span class="mspace thickspace"></span><span class="mord mathsf">i</span><span class="mord mathsf" style="margin-right: 0.06944em;">f</span></span><span class="mord"><span class="mspace thickspace"></span><span class="mord mathit">p</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit">x</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.03588em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">}</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf" style="margin-right: 0.06944em;">f</span><span class="mord mathsf">o</span><span class="mord mathsf" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">r</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">y</span><span class="mrel">←</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">v</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.03588em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">2</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mord"><span class="mspace thickspace"></span><span class="mord mathsf">i</span><span class="mord mathsf" style="margin-right: 0.06944em;">f</span></span><span class="mord"><span class="mspace thickspace"></span><span class="mord mathit">p</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">2</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit">x</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">2</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.03588em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">2</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">}</span><span class="mclose">⟩</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>which adds to the graph <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>⊗</mo><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>2</mn></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">g_1 \otimes g_2</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.58333em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.77777em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.03588em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mbin">⊗</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.03588em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">2</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> an edge from each vertex in <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo>{</mo><mi>v</mi><mo>∈</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">v</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>)</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">∣</mi><msub><mi>p</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>(</mo><mi>v</mi><mo>)</mo><mo>}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\{ v \in \mathsf{v}(g_1) | p_1(v) \}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">v</span><span class="mrel">∈</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">v</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.03588em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mord mathrm">∣</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit">p</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">v</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></span> to each vertex in <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo>{</mo><mi>v</mi><mo>∈</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">v</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>)</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">∣</mi><msub><mi>p</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>(</mo><mi>v</mi><mo>)</mo><mo>}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\{ v \in \mathsf{v}(g_2) | p_2(v) \}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">v</span><span class="mrel">∈</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">v</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.03588em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">2</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mord mathrm">∣</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit">p</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">2</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">v</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>When <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">∣</mi><mo>{</mo><mi>v</mi><mo>∈</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">v</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><msub><mi>g</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mo>)</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">∣</mi><msub><mi>p</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mo>(</mo><mi>v</mi><mo>)</mo><mo>}</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">∣</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">|\{ v \in \mathsf{v}(g_i) | p_i(v) \}| = 1</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathrm">∣</span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">v</span><span class="mrel">∈</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">v</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.311664em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.03588em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight">i</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mord mathrm">∣</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit">p</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.311664em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight">i</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">v</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mclose">}</span><span class="mord mathrm">∣</span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mord mathrm">1</span></span></span></span></span> then this form is the same as</p>
<p><span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo>⟨</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">l</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">t</mi></mrow><mspace width="0.277778em"></mspace><msub><mi>x</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>=</mo><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>[</mo><mn>0</mn><mo>]</mo><mspace width="0.277778em"></mspace><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">i</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">n</mi></mrow><mspace width="0.277778em"></mspace><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">l</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">t</mi></mrow><mspace width="0.277778em"></mspace><msub><mi>x</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>=</mo><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>[</mo><mn>0</mn><mo>]</mo><mspace width="0.277778em"></mspace><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">i</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">n</mi></mrow><mspace width="0.277778em"></mspace><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>⟩</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\langle \mathsf{let}\; x_1 = c_1[0] \; \mathsf{in}\; g_1 , \mathsf{let}\; x_2 = c_2[0] \; \mathsf{in}\; g_2 \rangle</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mopen">⟨</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">l</span><span class="mord mathsf">e</span><span class="mord mathsf">t</span></span><span class="mord"><span class="mspace thickspace"></span><span class="mord mathit">x</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit">c</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathrm">0</span><span class="mclose">]</span><span class="mord"><span class="mspace thickspace"></span><span class="mord mathsf">i</span><span class="mord mathsf">n</span></span><span class="mord"><span class="mspace thickspace"></span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.03588em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">l</span><span class="mord mathsf">e</span><span class="mord mathsf">t</span></span><span class="mord"><span class="mspace thickspace"></span><span class="mord mathit">x</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">2</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit">c</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">2</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathrm">0</span><span class="mclose">]</span><span class="mord"><span class="mspace thickspace"></span><span class="mord mathsf">i</span><span class="mord mathsf">n</span></span><span class="mord"><span class="mspace thickspace"></span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.03588em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">2</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">⟩</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>where <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>c</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mo>[</mo><mn>0</mn><mo>]</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">c_i[0]</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit">c</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.311664em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight">i</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathrm">0</span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span> denotes the singleton element inhabiting <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo>{</mo><mi>v</mi><mo>∈</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">v</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><msub><mi>g</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mo>)</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">∣</mi><msub><mi>p</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mo>(</mo><mi>v</mi><mo>)</mo><mo>}</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">∣</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\{ v \in \mathsf{v}(g_i) | p_i(v) \}|</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">v</span><span class="mrel">∈</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">v</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.311664em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.03588em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight">i</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mord mathrm">∣</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit">p</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.311664em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathit mtight">i</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">v</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mclose">}</span><span class="mord mathrm">∣</span></span></span></span></span>.</p>
<p>With this syntactic sugar we have a 1-line specification for the complete graph.</p>
<p><span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">c</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">o</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">m</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">p</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">l</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">t</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><mn>0</mn><mo>)</mo><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{complete}(0) = 0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">c</span><span class="mord mathsf">o</span><span class="mord mathsf">m</span><span class="mord mathsf">p</span><span class="mord mathsf">l</span><span class="mord mathsf">e</span><span class="mord mathsf">t</span><span class="mord mathsf">e</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathrm">0</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mord mathrm">0</span></span></span></span></span><br>
<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">c</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">o</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">m</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">p</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">l</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">t</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>)</mo><mo>=</mo><mo>⟨</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">f</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">o</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">r</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo>←</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">v</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">d</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">i</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">s</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">c</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">r</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">t</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi><mo>(</mo><mn mathvariant="sans-serif">1</mn><mo>)</mo></mrow><mo>)</mo><mo>)</mo><mo>{</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">d</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">i</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">s</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">c</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">r</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">t</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi><mo>(</mo><mn mathvariant="sans-serif">1</mn><mo>)</mo></mrow><mo>}</mo><mo separator="true">,</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">f</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">o</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">r</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>y</mi><mo>←</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">v</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">c</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">o</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">m</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">p</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">l</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">t</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>)</mo><mo>)</mo><mo>)</mo><mo>{</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">c</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">o</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">m</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">p</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">l</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">t</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>)</mo><mo>}</mo><mo>⟩</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{complete}(n) = \langle \mathsf{for} ( x \leftarrow \mathsf{v}(\mathsf{discrete(1)}))\{ \mathsf{discrete(1)} \}, \mathsf{for} ( y \leftarrow \mathsf{v}(\mathsf{complete}(n-1)))\{ \mathsf{complete}(n-1) \} \rangle</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em;
