<p>This gives rise to the graph of reductions of a term, <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">r</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">d</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>t</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{red}(t)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">r</span><span class="mord mathsf">e</span><span class="mord mathsf">d</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathit">t</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span> which is defined by</p>
<p><span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">r</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">d</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo>)</mo><mo>=</mo><mo>↑</mo><mi>x</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{red}(x) = \uparrow x</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">r</span><span class="mord mathsf">e</span><span class="mord mathsf">d</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathit">x</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mrel">↑</span><span class="mord mathit">x</span></span></span></span></span><br>
<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">r</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">d</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>λ</mi><mi>x</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mi>t</mi><mo>)</mo><mo>=</mo><mo>↑</mo><mo>(</mo><mi>λ</mi><mi>x</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mi>t</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{red}(\lambda x.t) = \uparrow (\lambda x.t)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">r</span><span class="mord mathsf">e</span><span class="mord mathsf">d</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathit">λ</span><span class="mord mathit">x</span><span class="mord mathrm">.</span><span class="mord mathit">t</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mrel">↑</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathit">λ</span><span class="mord mathit">x</span><span class="mord mathrm">.</span><span class="mord mathit">t</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span><br>
<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">r</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">d</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><mo>(</mo><mi>λ</mi><mi>x</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mi>t</mi><mo>)</mo><mi>u</mi><mo>)</mo><mo>=</mo><mo>⟨</mo><mo>↑</mo><mo>(</mo><mo>(</mo><mi>λ</mi><mi>x</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mi>t</mi><mo>)</mo><mi>u</mi><mo>)</mo><mo separator="true">,</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">r</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">d</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>t</mi><mo>[</mo><mi>u</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><mi>x</mi><mo>]</mo><mo>)</mo><mo>⟩</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{red}((\lambda x.t)u) = \langle \uparrow ((\lambda x.t)u),\mathsf{red}(t[u/x])\rangle</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">r</span><span class="mord mathsf">e</span><span class="mord mathsf">d</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathit">λ</span><span class="mord mathit">x</span><span class="mord mathrm">.</span><span class="mord mathit">t</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mord mathit">u</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mopen">⟨</span><span class="mrel">↑</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathit">λ</span><span class="mord mathit">x</span><span class="mord mathrm">.</span><span class="mord mathit">t</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mord mathit">u</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">r</span><span class="mord mathsf">e</span><span class="mord mathsf">d</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathit">t</span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathit">u</span><span class="mord mathrm">/</span><span class="mord mathit">x</span><span class="mclose">]</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mclose">⟩</span></span></span></span></span><br>
<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">r</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">d</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>t</mi><mi>u</mi><mo>)</mo><mo>=</mo><mo>⟨</mo><mo>↑</mo><mo>(</mo><mi>t</mi><mi>u</mi><mo>)</mo><mo separator="true">,</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">f</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">o</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">r</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><msup><mi>t</mi><mo mathvariant="normal">′</mo></msup><mo>←</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">v</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">r</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">d</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>t</mi><mo>)</mo><mo>)</mo><mo>{</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">r</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">d</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><msup><mi>t</mi><mo mathvariant="normal">′</mo></msup><mi>u</mi><mo>)</mo><mo>}</mo><mo>⟩</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{red}(tu) = \langle \uparrow (tu),\mathsf{for}( t' \leftarrow \mathsf{v}( \mathsf{red}(t) )\{\mathsf{red}(t'u)\}\rangle</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.751892em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1.00189em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">r</span><span class="mord mathsf">e</span><span class="mord mathsf">d</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathit">t</span><span class="mord mathit">u</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mopen">⟨</span><span class="mrel">↑</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathit">t</span><span class="mord mathit">u</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf" style="margin-right: 0.06944em;">f</span><span class="mord mathsf">o</span><span class="mord mathsf" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">r</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit">t</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.751892em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">′</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mrel">←</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">v</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">r</span><span class="mord mathsf">e</span><span class="mord mathsf">d</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathit">t</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">r</span><span class="mord mathsf">e</span><span class="mord mathsf">d</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit">t</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.751892em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">′</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord mathit">u</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mclose">}</span><span class="mclose">⟩</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>The ambitious reader is invited to provide a similar domain of graphs for the <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">r</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">h</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">o</mi></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{rho}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">r</span><span class="mord mathsf">h</span><span class="mord mathsf">o</span></span></span></span></span></span>-calculus.</p>
<h3 id="reflection-and-the-syntax-of-a-graph">Reflection and the syntax of a graph</h3>
<p>In some sense the entire point of the previous sections is to provide proof that the domain <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">G</mi></mrow><mo>[</mo><mi>X</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>V</mi><mo>]</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{G}[X,V]</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">G</span></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span> serves equally well as theory of variables or as a theory of vertices, provided that <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>X</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">X</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span></span></span></span></span> and <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>V</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">V</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span></span></span></span></span> serve those roles respectively. That is, <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">G</mi></mrow><mo>[</mo><mi>X</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>V</mi><mo>]</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{G}[X,V]</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">G</span></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span> comes with an effective procedure for deciding when a graph, say <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>g</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">g</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span></span></span></span></span> is in the domain,  <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">G</mi></mrow><mo>[</mo><mi>X</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>V</mi><mo>]</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{G}[X,V]</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">G</span></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span>. Specifically, we define <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>g</mi><mo>∈</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">G</mi></mrow><mo>[</mo><mi>X</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>V</mi><mo>]</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">g \in \mathsf{G}[X,V]</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="mrel">∈</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">G</span></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span> to be the determination that <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">G</mi></mrow><mo>[</mo><mi>X</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>V</mi><mo>]</mo><mo separator="true">;</mo><mo>(</mo><mo>)</mo><mo separator="true">;</mo><mo>(</mo><mo>)</mo><mo>⊢</mo><mi>g</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{G}[X,V];();() \vdash g</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">G</span></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="mclose">]</span><span class="mpunct">;</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mpunct">;</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mrel">⊢</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span></span></span></span></span>, i.e. that <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>g</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">g</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.43056em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span></span></span></span></span> is closed in <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">G</mi></mrow><mo>[</mo><mi>X</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>V</mi><mo>]</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{G}[X,V]</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">G</span></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span>. Likewise, <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">G</mi></mrow><mo>[</mo><mi>X</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>V</mi><mo>]</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{G}[X,V]</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">G</span></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span> comes with an effective procedure for determining if two graphs are equal. This observation yields additional expressive power. We can consider graph domains that are recursively defined.</p>
<p><span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">D</mi></mrow><mo>[</mo><mi>X</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>V</mi><mo>]</mo><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">G</mi></mrow><mo>[</mo><mi>X</mi><mo>+</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">D</mi></mrow><mo>[</mo><mi>X</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>V</mi><mo>]</mo><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>V</mi><mo>+</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">D</mi></mrow><mo>[</mo><mi>X</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>V</mi><mo>]</mo><mo>]</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{D}[X,V] = \mathsf{G}[X + \mathcal{D}[X,V],V + \mathcal{D}[X,V]]</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">D</span></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="mclose">]</span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">G</span></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">D</span></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="mclose">]</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">D</span></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="mclose">]</span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>Domains like <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">D</mi></mrow><mo>[</mo><mi>X</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>V</mi><mo>]</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{D}[X,V]</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">D</span></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span> allow us to create graphs in which we freely mix vertices from <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>V</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">V</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span></span></span></span></span> with vertices made out of entire graphs. As an example, with the recursive domain we given a graph <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>g</mi><mo>∈</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">G</mi></mrow><mo>[</mo><mi>X</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>V</mi><mo>]</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">g \in \mathsf{G}[X,V]</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="mrel">∈</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">G</span></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span> we can compute the graph of its syntax, <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">s</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>g</mi><mo>)</mo><mo>∈</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">D</mi></mrow><mo>[</mo><mi>X</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>V</mi><mo>]</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{s}(g) \in \mathcal{D}[X,V]</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">s</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mrel">∈</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">D</span></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span>.</p>
<p><span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">s</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><mn>0</mn><mo>)</mo><mo>=</mo><mo>┌</mo><mn>0</mn><mo>┐</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">∣</mi><mn>0</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{s}( 0 ) = \ulcorner 0 \urcorner | 0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">s</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathrm">0</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mopen amsrm">┌</span><span class="mord mathrm">0</span><span class="mclose amsrm">┐</span><span class="mord mathrm">∣</span><span class="mord mathrm">0</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p><span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">s</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>v</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">∣</mi><mi>g</mi><mo>)</mo><mo>=</mo><mo>(</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">l</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">t</mi></mrow><mspace mathvariant="sans-serif">n</mi></mrow><mspace width="0.277778em"></mspace><mo>┌</mo><mi>g</mi><mo>┐</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">∣</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">s</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>g</mi><mo>)</mo><mo separator="true">,</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">l</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">t</mi></mrow><mspace width="0.277778em"></mspace><mo>┌</mo><mi>v</mi><mo>┐</mo><mo>=</mo><mi>v</mi><mspace width="0.277778em"></mspace><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">i</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">n</mi></mrow><mspace width="0.277778em"></mspace><mo>┌</mo><mi>v</mi><mo>┐</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">∣</mi><mn>0</mn><mo>)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{s}( v | g ) =  (\mathsf{let}\; \ulcorner g \urcorner = g \; \mathsf{in}\; \ulcorner g \urcorner | \mathsf{s}(g),\mathsf{let}\; \ulcorner v \urcorner = v \; \mathsf{in}\; \ulcorner v \urcorner | 0)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">s</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">v</span><span class="mord mathrm">∣</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">l</span><span class="mord mathsf">e</span><span class="mord mathsf">t</span></span><span class="mopen amsrm"><span class="mspace thickspace"></span><span class="mopen amsrm">┌</span></span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="mclose amsrm">┐</span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="mord"><span class="mspace thickspace"></span><span class="mord mathsf">i</span><span class="mord mathsf">n</span></span><span class="mopen amsrm"><span class="mspace thickspace"></span><span class="mopen amsrm">┌</span></span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="mclose amsrm">┐</span><span class="mord mathrm">∣</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord class="mord mathsf">l</span><span class="mord mathsf">e</span><span class="mord mathsf">t</span></span><span class="mopen amsrm"><span class="mspace thickspace"></span><span class="mopen amsrm">┌</span></span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">v</span><span class="mclose amsrm">┐</span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">v</span><span class="mord"><span class="mspace thickspace"></span><span class="mord mathsf">i</span><span class="mord mathsf">n</span></span><span class="mopen amsrm"><span class="mspace thickspace"></span><span class="mopen amsrm">┌</span></span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">v</span><span class="mclose amsrm">┐</span><span class="mord mathrm">∣</span><span class="mord mathrm">0</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>$\mathsf{s}( g_1 \otimes g_2 ) $<br>
<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo>=</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">=</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.36687em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.36687em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mrel">=</span></span></span></span></span><br>
<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo>(</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">l</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">t</mi></mrow><mspace width="0.277778em"></mspace><mo>┌</mo><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>┐</mo><mo>=</mo><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mspace width="0.277778em"></mspace><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">i</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">n</mi></mrow><mspace width="0.277778em"></mspace><mo>┌</mo><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>┐</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">∣</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">s</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>)</mo><mo separator="true">,</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">l</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">t</mi></mrow><mspace width="0.277778em"></mspace><mo>┌</mo><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>┐</mo><mo>=</mo><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mspace width="0.277778em"></mspace><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">i</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">n</mi></mrow><mspace width="0.277778em"></mspace><mo>┌</mo><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>┐</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">∣</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">s</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>)</mo><mo>)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">(\mathsf{let}\; \ulcorner g_1 \urcorner = g_1 \; \mathsf{in}\; \ulcorner g_1 \urcorner | \mathsf{s}(g_1),\mathsf{let}\; \ulcorner g_2 \urcorner = g_2 \; \mathsf{in}\; \ulcorner g_2 \urcorner | \mathsf{s}(g_2))</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; <p><span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">s</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">l</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">t</mi></mrow><mspace width="0.277778em"></mspace><mi>x</mi><mo>=</mo><mi>v</mi><mspace width="0.277778em"></mspace><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">i</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">n</mi></mrow><mspace width="0.277778em"></mspace><mi>g</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{s}( \mathsf{let}\; x = v \;\mathsf{in}\; g )</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">s</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">l</span><span class="mord mathsf">e</span><span class="mord mathsf">t</span></span><span class="mord mathit"><span class="mspace thickspace"></span><span class="mord mathit">x</span></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">v</span><span class="mord"><span class="mspace thickspace"></span><span class="mord mathsf">i</span><span class="mord mathsf">n</span></span><span class="mord mathit"><span class="mspace thickspace"></span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span><br>
$ = $<br>
$  (\mathsf{let}; \ulcorner g \urcorner = g ; \mathsf{in}; \ulcorner g \urcorner  | \mathsf{s}(g),\mathsf{let}; \ulcorner x \urcorner = x ; \mathsf{in}; \mathsf{let} ; \ulcorner v \urcorner = v ; \mathsf{in}; \ulcorner x \urcorner | \ulcorner v \urcorner | 0)$</p>

<p>It is easy to see that <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">S</mi><mo>[</mo><mi mathvariant="script">X</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi mathvariant="script">V</mi><mo>]</mo><mo>=</mo><mo>{</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">s</mi></mrow><mo>(</mo><mi>g</mi><mo>)</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">∣</mi><mi>g</mi><mo>∈</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">D</mi></mrow><mo>[</mo><mi mathvariant="script">X</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi mathvariant="script">V</mi><mo>]</mo><mo>}</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{S[X,V] = \{ \mathsf{s}(g) | g \in \mathcal{D}[X,V] \}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right: 0.075em;">S</span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right: 0.14643em;">X</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right: 0.08222em;">V</span><span class="mclose">]</span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">s</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mord mathrm">∣</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="mrel">∈</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">D</span></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right: 0.14643em;">X</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right: 0.08222em;">V</span><span class="mclose">]</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></span></span> is a subtype of <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">D</mi></mrow><mo>[</mo><mi>X</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>V</mi><mo>]</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{D}[X,V]</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">D</span></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span>.</p>
<p>And given the syntax of a graph we can always recover the original graph.</p>
<h2 id="ladl-and-graphs">LADL and Graphs</h2>
<p>We can apply the <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">L</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">A</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">D</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">L</mi></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{LADL}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">L</span><span class="mord mathsf">A</span><span class="mord mathsf">D</span><span class="mord mathsf">L</span></span></span></span></span></span> procedure to the theory of graphs. When the collection is a set then the types are given as</p>

class="mrel">=</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">v</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.03588em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">2</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord"><span class="mspace thickspace"></span><span class="mord mathsf">i</span><span class="mord mathsf">n</span></span><span class="mord mathit"><span class="mspace thickspace"></span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">ψ</span></span><span class="mclose">⟩</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>This sets up our foundational investigation. Recall that our examples <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">d</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">i</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">s</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">c</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">r</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">t</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{discrete}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">d</span><span class="mord mathsf">i</span><span class="mord mathsf">s</span><span class="mord mathsf">c</span><span class="mord mathsf" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">r</span><span class="mord mathsf">e</span><span class="mord mathsf">t</span><span class="mord mathsf">e</span></span></span></span></span></span>, <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">c</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">h</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">a</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">i</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">n</mi></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{chain}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">c</span><span class="mord mathsf">h</span><span class="mord mathsf">a</span><span class="mord mathsf">i</span><span class="mord mathsf">n</span></span></span></span></span></span>, <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">c</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">y</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">c</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">l</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{cycle}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.88888em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">c</span><span class="mord mathsf" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">y</span><span class="mord mathsf">c</span><span class="mord mathsf">l</span><span class="mord mathsf">e</span></span></span></span></span></span>, and <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">c</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">o</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">m</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">p</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">l</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">t</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">e</mi></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{complete}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.88888em; vertical-align: -0.19444em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">c</span><span class="mord mathsf">o</span><span class="mord mathsf">m</span><span class="mord mathsf">p</span><span class="mord mathsf">l</span><span class="mord mathsf">e</span><span class="mord mathsf">t</span><span class="mord mathsf">e</span></span></span></span></span></span> gave rise to subtypes of <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">G</mi></mrow><mo>[</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">N</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">a</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">t</mi></mrow><mo separator="true">,</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">N</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">a</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">t</mi></mrow><mo>]</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{G}[\mathsf{Nat},\mathsf{Nat}]</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">G</span></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">N</span><span class="mord mathsf">a</span><span class="mord mathsf">t</span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">N</span><span class="mord mathsf">a</span><span class="mord mathsf">t</span></span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span> by exploiting structure of <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">N</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">a</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">t</mi></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{Nat}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">N</span><span class="mord mathsf">a</span><span class="mord mathsf">t</span></span></span></span></span></span>. Similarly, the <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">L</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">A</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">D</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">L</mi></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{LADL}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">L</span><span class="mord mathsf">A</span><span class="mord mathsf">D</span><span class="mord mathsf">L</span></span></span></span></span></span> types give rise to subtypes of <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">G</mi></mrow><mo>[</mo><mi>X</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>V</mi><mo>]</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{G}[X,V]</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">G</span></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span>. Our focus of investigation is the question of the conditions under which the structure of <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>X</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">X</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span></span></span></span></span> and <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>V</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">V</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span></span></span></span></span> supply subtypes of <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">G</mi></mrow><mo>[</mo><mi>X</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>V</mi><mo>]</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{G}[X,V]</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">G</span></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span> that coincide with the <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">L</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">A</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">D</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">L</mi></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{LADL}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">L</span><span class="mord mathsf">A</span><span class="mord mathsf">D</span><span class="mord mathsf">L</span></span></span></span></span></span> types?</p>
<p>Not surprisingly, we find that when we can faithfully map <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>X</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">X</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span></span></span></span></span> (resp., <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>V</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">V</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span></span></span></span></span>) into <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">G</mi></mrow><mo>[</mo><msup><mi>X</mi><mo mathvariant="normal">′</mo></msup><mo separator="true">,</mo><msup><mi>V</mi><mo mathvariant="normal">′</mo></msup><mo>]</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{G}[X',V']</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.751892em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1.00189em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">G</span></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.751892em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">′</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.751892em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">′</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span> for some <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>X</mi><mo mathvariant="normal">′</mo></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">X'</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.751892em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.751892em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.751892em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">′</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> and <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi>V</mi><mo mathvariant="normal">′</mo></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">V'</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.751892em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.751892em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.751892em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">′</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>, then we can establish an isomorphism between the subtypes available from the structure of <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>X</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">X</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span></span></span></span></span> and <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>V</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">V</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span></span></span></span></span> and the <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">L</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">A</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">D</mi><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">L</mi></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{LADL}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.69444em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.69444em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">L</span><span class="mord mathsf">A</span><span class="mord mathsf">D</span><span class="mord mathsf">L</span></span></span></span></span></span> types. This observation sets up a process by which domains of <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>X</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">X</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span></span></span></span></span> and <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mi>V</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">V</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span></span></span></span></span> are replaced by graph-based representations of them. The limit of this process, the smallest structure for which these coincide, is given by</p>
<p><span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">D</mi></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">G</mi></mrow><mo>[</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>+</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">D</mi></mrow><mo separator="true">,</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>+</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">D</mi></mrow><mo>]</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{D} = \mathsf{G}[1 + \mathcal{D},1 + \mathcal{D}]</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">D</span></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">G</span></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathrm">1</span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">D</span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mord mathrm">1</span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">D</span></span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>This domain is the least witness of the microcosm principle applied to the domain of graphs.</p>
<h3 id="categories">Categories</h3>
<p>We can provide a theory of categories, <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">C</mi></mrow><mo>[</mo><mi>X</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>V</mi><mo>]</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{C}[X,V]</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right: 0.05834em;">C</span></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span>, that are subdomains of <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">G</mi></mrow><mo>[</mo><mi>X</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>V</mi><mo>]</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{G}[X,V]</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">G</span></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span>.  In point of fact, given the discussion above we can identify a subtype of <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">G</mi></mrow><mo>[</mo><mi>X</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>V</mi><mo>]</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{G}[X,V]</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">G</span></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span> in which the edges between any two vertices enjoy the structure given by <span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">D</mi></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{D}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.68333em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.68333em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">D</span></span></span></span></span></span>.  This gives us a domain equation for an infinity category.</p>
<h2 id="miscellaneous-operations">Miscellaneous operations</h2>
<p><span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">G</mi><mo>∘</mo></msup><mo>[</mo><mi>X</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>V</mi><mo>]</mo><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">G</mi></mrow><mo>[</mo><mi>V</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>X</mi><mo>]</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{G}^{\circ}[X,V] = \mathsf{G}[V,X]</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">G</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.724115em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">∘</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="mclose">]</span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">G</span></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span></span><br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">G</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">V</mi></mrow></msup><mo>[</mo><mi>X</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>V</mi><mo>]</mo><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">G</mi></mrow><mo>[</mo><mi>V</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>V</mi><mo>]</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{G}^{\mathsf{V}}[X,V] = \mathsf{G}[V,V]</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.899108em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1.14911em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">G</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.899108em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathsf mtight" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">V</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="mclose">]</span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">G</span></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span></span><br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><msup><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">G</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">X</mi></mrow></msup><mo>[</mo><mi>X</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>V</mi><mo>]</mo><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">G</mi></mrow><mo>[</mo><mi>X</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>X</mi><mo>]</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{G}^{\mathsf{X}}[X,V] = \mathsf{G}[X,X]</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.899108em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1.14911em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord"><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">G</span></span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.899108em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.113em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathsf mtight">X</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="mclose">]</span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">G</span></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span></span><br>
<span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">G</mi></mrow><mo>[</mo><msub><mi>X</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>V</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>]</mo><mo>+</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">G</mi></mrow><mo>[</mo><msub><mi>X</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>V</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>]</mo><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">G</mi></mrow><mo>[</mo><msub><mi>X</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>+</mo><msub><mi>X</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>V</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>+</mo><msub><mi>V</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>]</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{G}[X_1,V_1] +  \mathsf{G}[X_2,V_2] = \mathsf{G}[X_1+X_2,V_1 + V_2]</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; <span class="katex--display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">G</mi></mrow><mo>[</mo><msub><mi>X</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>V</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>]</mo><mo>⋅</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">G</mi></mrow><mo>[</mo><msub><mi>X</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>V</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>]</mo><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="sans-serif">G</mi></mrow><mo>[</mo><msub><mi>X</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>+</mo><msub><mi>V</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>X</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>+</mo><msub><mi>V</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>]</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathsf{G}[X_1,V_1] \cdot  \mathsf{G}[X_2,V_2] = \mathsf{G}[X_1 + V_1,X_2 + V_2]</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.75em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 1em; margin-left: -0.22222em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">]</span><span class="mbin">⋅</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">G</span></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.07847em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">2</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.22222em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">2</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">]</span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathsf">G</span></span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.07847em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.22222em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">X</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.07847em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">2</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathit" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.301108em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.22222em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">2</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>Note that the crossover style operations like “<span class="katex--inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math><semantics><mrow><mo>⋅</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\cdot</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.44445em;"></span><span class="strut bottom" style="height: 0.44445em; vertical-align: 0em;"></span><span class="base"><span class="mord">⋅</span></span></span></span></span>” together with reflection allow us to define <em>evolutionary</em> processes (in the sense of Holland) for graphs and graph domains. The principal missing ingredient is a fitness function for evaluating graphs and graph domains for selection and “reproduction.”</p>
<p>[This is a reference test][Holland]</p>

<h1 id="casper-components">Casper components</h1>
